| <span data-ttu-id="ba675-1093">Entrada</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba675-1093">Entry</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="ba675-1094">Value</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba675-1094">Value</span></span> |
